I commented out the last bit since none of the sequences match because of what could be a variety of reasons, probably some combination of how I wasn't sure how to edit a dictionary value when the keys were set as a tuple and what I was using as an amino acid code. 

By the time I realized I had no idea how to work with a tuple dictionary and no one on the internet did either, it was too late to go back and just make my own code instead of using what Gibas posted. I ended up trying to make entirely different dictionaries out of it all and work from that, and honestly I'm suprised this nonsense even looks like it works.
